< Review>
This place gets the job done with a traditional soa brush wash and rinse. I don't recommend the contactless soap spray option as the times I have used them they don't really get a good mix of soap to water. The drying station that follows after the wash occasionally has people taking their time or just waiting for something so be prepared to either dry off behind them as they sit and wait for the water to evaporate or drive to the sides of any other drying station. Most of the time they have an attendant there with a bright orange shirt who is helpful in breaking larger bills for 1's,5's,and 10's.<//Review>

Mittapheap means friendship/friendliness...

We are travelers and we came to this restaurant per Google's recommendation. Thanks Google. < Review>
Store staff are great, but they are let down by the parent company (or whoever manages their web site).  The Santa Barbara store web site indicates the store stocks golf shoes.  I drove ~ 40 miles to the store on State Street to be told they stock no golf shoes.  I guess I should have telephoned first to be certain, but since the web site was so specific, I assumed golf shoes would be available.  Ironically, the advertising video playing on the large TV in the store highlighted how good the Skechers golf shoes are.  I guess I have to buy them on-line to find out.  I did buy a pair of walking shoes, so at least the trip was not a complete waste of time.< /Review>

< text>
Unless you are going for the promo, do not go in late in the day after a promo. IHOP was offering a free stack of pancakes today if you donated to a charity. 7am-7pm on all the promotions. This location apparently ended theirs at 2pm. Okay, no biggie. I missed out. Giant posters offering a limited time all you can eat pancakes with the purchase of an omelette. Well that sounds like a great deal. I order the steak omelette. It came out fairly quick and tasted great to me.
The problem is the staff after a promotion. They probably brought more staff in to handle the promo but everyone was beleaguered. My server more so than others. Appeared to rush my initial order and came with my check after I had finished my omelette and pancakes. I had to request more pancakes which surprised him but he agreed to get me another 2. It took awhile which I could understand. It came out great. But that was it. My server did not seem to come down my aisle again or check up on me. Did not get a refill on water once or offered any more of the unlimited pancakes. He unfortunately did not identify himself, turned quickly when I tried to look at his name tag, and was not the server listed on my check.

Can‚Äôt say I blame the staff but do yourself a favor and not go in after a promo. The food was still good but everyone looked battle weary and customer service seemed to suffer.< /text>
